 is

 a post shared byactor pankaj tripathi (@ pankajtri3fanclub) onsep 12, 2018 at 7:36 am pdtview this post on Instagram There are two ways in life
 ek bahati dhara ke saath bahna or doosraa dhaaraon ke saath panga lenaa or apane raste khud bananaa
 i got a lot of offers after Gangs of Wasseypur
 un sabhi filmon main mere haath me bandook hi hote
 But Ashwini Iyer ji showed me the way of screwing
 bandook ke thik baad mere haath me chok or duster tha
 The film was Neil Batte Sannata
 ek kalakaar ke taur par alag alag charitra par kaam karnaa chunauti ke saath romaanchak bhi hota he
 It was about to open new avenues for me as an artist
 ye panga tha
 Screwed by the image of Sultan Qureshi with the gun
 ashvini ke saath milakar hamane aglaa panga liya ek khule pankh vaali beti ke pita ke rup main
 Bitti's father as Narottam Mishra
 is baar panga tha ek roodhiwaadee samaaj ke khilaaf
 This film used to teach how to laugh, to laugh at daughters
 bareli kii barfi thi ye
 Working with Ashwini has always been like new expectations, opening new doors as an artist
 aap swayan ko or behatar taur pe explor karte ho
 You will mess with yourself and your own boundaries
 unke har film main kaam karnaa mere liye meraa khud se kiya hua ek adrishy qaraar he
 And i have always believed that when you are like a family, every job gives satisfaction
 or jab aapkaa parivaar aapke saath hota he to ji zindagi se panga lenaa aasaan ho jaataa he
 This time we are taking Panga directly from Panga
 hamaari agali film 'panga' ke rup main
 Best wishes to the entire 'panga' team

 jammu-kashmir kii anantnag loksabhaa seat par kadi suraksha ke bich teen charnon ke tahat somvaar ko antim charan kii voting sampann hui
 In the Lok Sabha elections in 2019, former Chief Minister Mehbooba Mufti is again in the fray to win the election of MP from Anantnag Lok Sabha seat
 somvaar ko kulgaam jila ke chaar vidhansabha kshetron- nurabad, devsar, kulgaam or homashalibag main bhi vot daale gaye
 Anantnag seat recorded around 10 percent polling till 5 pm
 rajya kii anantnag loksabhaa seat par pidipi or neshnal conference ke bich kaante kaa muqabla hota rahaa he
 BJP candidates from this seat in Jammu and Kashmir are not able to save even their bail
 loksabhaa chunaav 2019 main anantnag loksabhaa seat par pidipi se purv mukhyamantri mahabuuba mufti phir se empi kaa chunaav jeetne ke liye maidan main hai
 They face Hasan Masoodi of the National Conference
 congress ne gulam ahamed mir to vahiin bijepi ne sophy yusuf ko khadaa kiya he
 Political equation of seat Anantnag Lok Sabha seat of Jammu and Kashmir is important in many ways
 2014 main is seat par rajya kii purv mukhyamantri mahabuuba mufti ne jeet darj kii thi, lekin unke istife ke do saal tak is seat par upachunaav nahin ho sakaa, iske peeche ghati main ashaanti kaa maahaul jimmedaar he
 If you look at the figures of the Election Commission, it is the seat that remains the longest vacant in 1996 after the by-law in six months
 is seat se mahabuuba ke alaava pidipi adhyaksh rahe mufti mohammad said or congress ke varisht netaa rahe mohammad shafi kuraishi bhi saansad ban chuke hai
 This seat is the stronghold of PDP
 2014 main hue vidhansabha chunaavon main anantnag kii 16 vidhansabha siton main se 11 siton par pidipi jiti thi
 Political background Mohammad Shafi Qureshi, one of the senior Congress leaders, won the Anantnag seat in 1967
 vah teen baar (1967, 71 or 77) lagaataar saansad rahe
 After this the seat went to the part of Jammu Kashmir National Conference
 1980 main neshnal conference ke gulam rasul kochak, 1984 main neshnal conference ke begum akbar jahaan abdulla or 1989 main neshnal conference ke hi piel handu saansad bane
 In the elections held in 1996, Mohammad Maqbool MP was elected from this seat on a Janata Dal ticket
 iske baad 1998 main congress ke tikat par mufti mohammad said jeetne main kaamyaab hue
 In 1999, this seat again came to the National Conference and Ali Mohammad Naik became MP

 ) The Akhil Bharatiya Vidyarthi Parishad (ABVP) has won three out of four posts in the Delhi University Students Union (DUSU) election
